# Phase-Transition Sweep

This artifact sweeps explicit bit budgets against exact contract state spaces.
It compares positional bit-geometry schemes with trace-based clustering baselines.

Schemes:

- `prefix`: Keep the first B bits of the canonical binary code.
- `suffix`: Keep the last B bits of the canonical binary code.
- `interleaved`: Keep B bits from a deterministic high-low interleaving of bit positions.
- `cluster_answer`: Cluster states by answer traces first, then refine within each answer block by full joint traces.
- `cluster_witness`: Cluster states by witness traces first, then refine within each witness block by full joint traces.
- `cluster_joint`: Cluster states directly by full joint answer/witness traces.

Policies:

- `breach`: abstain on mixed buckets.
- `forced`: emit a majority answer and majority witness.

## Highlights

- The exact turn-on point is unchanged by code geometry: `prefix` -> `M_3` at `4` bits, `Q_(3,2)` at `6` bits, `suffix` -> `M_3` at `4` bits, `Q_(3,2)` at `6` bits, `interleaved` -> `M_3` at `4` bits, `Q_(3,2)` at `6` bits.
- The pre-threshold mirage shelf survives all three geometries for `Q_(5,3)` at `9` bits: `prefix`: acc `0.999` / witness `0.987`, `suffix`: acc `0.909` / witness `0.733`, `interleaved`: acc `0.995` / witness `0.970`.
- The causal referee shelf also survives the geometry change at `3` bits: `prefix`: acc `1.000` / witness `0.740`, `suffix`: acc `0.970` / witness `0.970`, `interleaved`: acc `0.992` / witness `0.882`.
- The trace-clustering baselines are more discriminating than the bit geometries: `cluster_answer` on `Q_(5,3)` at `9` bits gives acc `1.000` / witness `1.000`, `cluster_witness` on `Q_(5,3)` at `9` bits gives acc `1.000` / witness `1.000`, `cluster_joint` on `Q_(5,3)` at `9` bits gives acc `1.000` / witness `1.000`.
- On the realistic causal corpus, the clustering baselines remain subexact at the same pre-threshold point: `cluster_answer` on `causal_referee` at `3` bits gives acc `1.000` / witness `0.948`, `cluster_witness` on `causal_referee` at `3` bits gives acc `0.975` / witness `0.970`, `cluster_joint` on `causal_referee` at `3` bits gives acc `0.988` / witness `0.976`.
- Reading the two lines together, the current right-context probe bank is strong enough to expose a causal mirage shelf, but not yet separator-complete for the full two-sided synthetic quotient under joint trace clustering.

## Families

- `M_1`: `5` exact states, threshold `2.322` bits. Exact two-sided bare threshold quotient. Probe-joint `3` / probe-answer `3`.
- `M_2`: `9` exact states, threshold `3.170` bits. Exact two-sided bare threshold quotient. Probe-joint `4` / probe-answer `4`.
- `M_3`: `14` exact states, threshold `3.807` bits. Exact two-sided bare threshold quotient. Probe-joint `5` / probe-answer `5`.
- `M_4`: `20` exact states, threshold `4.322` bits. Exact two-sided bare threshold quotient. Probe-joint `6` / probe-answer `6`.
- `M_5`: `27` exact states, threshold `4.755` bits. Exact two-sided bare threshold quotient. Probe-joint `7` / probe-answer `7`.
- `Q_(1,1)`: `5` exact states, threshold `2.322` bits. Protected-witness quotient with exact shift-and-max composition. Probe-joint `3` / probe-answer `3`.
- `Q_(2,1)`: `9` exact states, threshold `3.170` bits. Protected-witness quotient with exact shift-and-max composition. Probe-joint `4` / probe-answer `4`.
- `Q_(3,1)`: `14` exact states, threshold `3.807` bits. Protected-witness quotient with exact shift-and-max composition. Probe-joint `5` / probe-answer `5`.
- `Q_(4,1)`: `20` exact states, threshold `4.322` bits. Protected-witness quotient with exact shift-and-max composition. Probe-joint `6` / probe-answer `6`.
- `Q_(5,1)`: `27` exact states, threshold `4.755` bits. Protected-witness quotient with exact shift-and-max composition. Probe-joint `7` / probe-answer `7`.
- `Q_(1,2)`: `13` exact states, threshold `3.700` bits. Protected-witness quotient with exact shift-and-max composition. Probe-joint `5` / probe-answer `3`.
- `Q_(2,2)`: `29` exact states, threshold `4.858` bits. Protected-witness quotient with exact shift-and-max composition. Probe-joint `6` / probe-answer `4`.
- `Q_(3,2)`: `54` exact states, threshold `5.755` bits. Protected-witness quotient with exact shift-and-max composition. Probe-joint `7` / probe-answer `5`.
- `Q_(4,2)`: `90` exact states, threshold `6.492` bits. Protected-witness quotient with exact shift-and-max composition. Probe-joint `8` / probe-answer `6`.
- `Q_(5,2)`: `139` exact states, threshold `7.119` bits. Protected-witness quotient with exact shift-and-max composition. Probe-joint `9` / probe-answer `7`.
- `Q_(1,3)`: `35` exact states, threshold `5.129` bits. Protected-witness quotient with exact shift-and-max composition. Probe-joint `9` / probe-answer `3`.
- `Q_(2,3)`: `99` exact states, threshold `6.629` bits. Protected-witness quotient with exact shift-and-max composition. Probe-joint `10` / probe-answer `4`.
- `Q_(3,3)`: `224` exact states, threshold `7.807` bits. Protected-witness quotient with exact shift-and-max composition. Probe-joint `11` / probe-answer `5`.
- `Q_(4,3)`: `440` exact states, threshold `8.781` bits. Protected-witness quotient with exact shift-and-max composition. Probe-joint `12` / probe-answer `6`.
- `Q_(5,3)`: `783` exact states, threshold `9.613` bits. Protected-witness quotient with exact shift-and-max composition. Probe-joint `13` / probe-answer `7`.
- `causal_referee`: `15` empirical support states, threshold `3.907` bits. Static sweep over the 89,291 unique-minimal referee narratives. The answer channel is adjustment-set size `k`; witness fidelity tracks exact named adjustment-set identity. Probe-joint `15` / probe-answer `4`. Canonical `Q_(k,k)` upper-bound support across the observed `k` values: `2532` states / `11.306` bits.
